	var addEvent = function(evt, handler) {
		if (window.addEventListener) {
			document.addEventListener(evt, handler, false);
		} else if (window.attachEvent) {
			document.attachEvent('on' + evt, handler);
		}
	};
	var removeEvent = function(evt, handler) {
		if (window.removeEventListener) {
			document.removeEventListener(evt, handler, false);
		} else if (window.detachEvent) {
			document.detachEvent('on' + evt, handler);
		}
	};
	var evts = 'contextmenu dblclick drag dragend dragenter dragleave dragover dragstart drop keydown keypress keyup mousedown mousemove mouseout mouseover mouseup mousewheel scroll'.split(' ');
	var logHuman = function() {
		var wfscr = document.createElement('script');
		wfscr.type = 'text/javascript';
		wfscr.async = true;
		wfscr.src = url + '&r=' + Math.random();
		(document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0]||document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0]).appendChild(wfscr);
		for (var i = 0; i < evts.length; i++) {
			removeEvent(evts[i], logHuman);
		}
	};
	for (var i = 0; i < evts.length; i++) {
		addEvent(evts[i], logHuman);
	}
})('//www.jaggaer.com/?wordfence_lh=1&hid=0B7048D53CC8AD7A6BE280B7A25B231C');

		<div class="wpb_wrapper">
			<p>JAGGAER has developed a highly engineered, comprehensive suite of spend management solutions because industries and organizations have unique challenges that cannot be met by a one size-fits-all approach. Powered by advanced analytics and the world’s most engaged supplier network, JAGGAER is the partner of choice for the world’s leading companies and institutions, from manufacturers to the public sector, and universities. JAGGAER is the world’s only company delivering best-of-breed solutions to manage the entire procurement spectrum, from indirect to direct spend.</p>
<p>Powered by a unique supplier-centered approach, JAGGAER provides the visibility, insight, transparency, and technology to rev up your procurement initiatives and decisions. Let a JAGGAER representative demonstrate exactly how our industry leading solutions can change your business.</p>

	<script type="text/javascript">

		jQuery(document).ready(function($) {

			$("#checkPriv").on("change", function(){
				if(this.checked) {
					$("#gated_form_button").attr("disabled", false);
		    } else {
					$("#gated_form_button").attr("disabled", true);
				}
			});

			$("#promoCheck").on("change", function(){
				// console.log($("#promoCheck:checkbox:checked").val());
			});
			$(document).on( 'click', '#fieldname24_1', function(e) {

				//ROI Form Updates

				if($('.roi-form-container').length > 0){

					//get ROI form values

					var totalspend = $('#fieldname12_1').val();

					var spendcontract = $('#fieldname13_1').val();

					var spendnoncontract = $('#fieldname14_1').val();

					var purchaseorders = $('#fieldname15_1').val();

					var nonpurchaseorders = $('#fieldname16_1').val();

					var numberinvoices = $('#fieldname17_1').val();



					//add ROI values on contact form

					$('input[name="total-spend"]').val(totalspend);

					$('input[name="spend-contract"]').val(spendcontract);

					$('input[name="spend-non-contract"]').val(spendnoncontract);

					$('input[name="purchase-orders"]').val(purchaseorders);

					$('input[name="non-purchase-orders"]').val(nonpurchaseorders);

					$('input[name="number-invoices"]').val(numberinvoices);

				}

			});



			document.addEventListener( 'wpcf7mailsent', function( event ) {

			    ga( 'send', 'event', 'Contact Form', 'submit' );

			}, false );



			$(document).on( 'click', '#gated_form_button', function(e) {

        e.preventDefault();

        $('.gated-form-loader').fadeIn();

        $('label.error').remove();
        // console.log($('#yourCountry option:checked').val());
				// console.log($("#promoCheck").val());
				var infoCheckbox;
				if($('#promoCheck').is(':checked')) {

					infoCheckbox = $("#promoCheck:checkbox:checked").val();
				} else {
					infoCheckbox = "";
				}
				if($('#yourCountry').val()) {
					console.log($('#yourCountry').val());
					$('label.error').remove();
				} else {
					console.log("new");
					$('.country').append('<label class="error">Please provide <strong>Country</strong></label>')
				}

				var data = {

					action: 'submit_gated_form',

					post_id: '473',

					firstName: $('#firstName').val(),

					lastName: $('#lastName').val(),

					email: $('#email').val(),

					phone: $('#phone').val(),

					title: $('#title').val(),

					yourCountry: $('#yourCountry').val(),

					company: $('#company').val(),

					formtype: $('#formtype').val(),

					resourcetype: $('#resourcetype').val(),

					infoCheck: infoCheckbox,

					document_location: window.location.href,

				};

				// since 2.8 ajaxurl is always defined in the admin header and points to admin-ajax.php

				$.post( 'https://www.jaggaer.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', data, function( response ) {

					if(response){

						$('.gated-form-loader').fadeOut();

						var responseobj = JSON.parse(response);

						if(responseobj.status == 'success'){

							//ga( 'send', 'event', 'Contact Form', 'submit' );

							if(responseobj.reload_page == 'yes'){

								window.location.reload();

							}else{

								// $('.gated_form').html(responseobj.download_link);

								$('.gated_form').html('<center>Thanks for your submission.</center>');

								window.location = responseobj.download_link;

							}

						}else{

							$.each(responseobj.errors, function( key, value ) {

								$('.form-row.'+key).append('<label class="error">'+value+'</label>');

							});

						}

					}

				});

	        });

		});

	</script>
